I come here when I really need to get the knots and tension released from my aching shoulders, back and neck. You won't find a better deal than here. 2 full hours for only $110! if you pay in cash. It's not as relaxing of an environment like a resort spa with the thin walls but it is still awesome. I prefer really strong hands and Sally has that kind of touch. She did a full hour on my shoulders and back then another hour for the rest of my body. I highly recommend it if your body is aching. You will definitely leave feeling better!< /review>

<UserId.>110548416478127016153</UserId.>< Review>
My friend and I stayed at the nearby hotel America's Best Value Inn while on a road trip from Oregon going into San Fransisco. While we stayed at the Value Inn we saw Murillo's next door. Without having to drive anywhere and a short walk, we decided on going to Murillo's for cold beers, margaritas, chips/salsa and dinner. It was everything that we were looking for. Basic overall. The interior was your traditional Mex. theme going on, cantina area to hang out in. As it was super hot out the day we were there, the cold beers and the flavored margaritas hit the spot. The food was fairly basic, but it served its need while we were living on the road.< /Review>

4</rating>
< Text>
I love this place! Great authentic Mexican food. Owned and operated by a local family. There are two locations. The original is in the downtown area of Vacaville and parking can  be a little tight the other location is much larger and has plenty of parking in the back. It is right off the freeway near the famous Nut Tree and even RVs would be able to park in the back. I am an extreme Mexican food fan and Murrillos is one of my favorite spots. The dinner menu is awesome and the combo plates let you try up to three different items in one plate. The mini paco is amazingly large and delicious. The Jalisco burrito is awesome but it doesn't come with rice and beans sadly. The lunch menu is not as good a value. I ordered enchilada lunch and a coke. It came to over 12.oo and it came with only 1 enchilada. First time I have ever left hungry. Go for dinner NOT A GOOD LUNCH STOP Chips and salsa are great and home made. Interestingly that hot salsa is served cold and the mild salsa is served warm.< /Text>

<Text>So I had to make another trip and try lunch, and was not dissatisfied at all.  Service was just as prompt, friendly and courteous as it was for dinner.   Portions remained good size, meal was again served quickly and piping hot.  The enchiladas we're as close to a Tex-Mex that I grew up eating and so I would definitely recommend sitting down and trying a meal.  Staff is friendly, family owned and take great care in treating their patron's well.  I've had both lunch and dinner and no matter which time they remain consistent with both quality and service.

Had a nice dinner, went in about 5:30, and was able to get a table on this Saturday.   Good service, good good, nice portions for the value.  Served with chips and salsa, both regular and spicy. I had a combination plate, 2 items, with the enchilada (beef) which was delicious, and a chilli relleno which was good, served with rice and beans. Food was served extremely prompt and was served piping hot.  My server was courteous, prompt and polite, and it was packed at the time I had dinner.  If in the area it's a good place to dine. Restaurant was clean, and practice safe protocol, and staff all wore mask.<//Text><user>117672440790907738243< /user></record>
